 G53 DO YOU HAVE ANY VIEWS OR OBSERVATIONS ON THE WAY THE INCIDENT WAS HANDLED

 AFTER THE MATCH WAS STOPPED?

 I THINK THE POLICE WERE TOTALLY DISORGANISED, THEY SEEMED TO THINK THAT THERE

 WAS SOME QORT OF DISORDER IN THE TERRACING WHEN FANS WERE CLIMBING OVER THE

 FENCE SO THEY LINED UP ACROSS THE HALF WAY LINE AND THE NORTH STAND AS IF TO

^ - G R E G A T E THE SUPPORTERS.   THEY DIDN'T KNOW WHAT WAS GOING ON.   THERE SEEMED

 O B E     A LACK OF LEADERSHIP     IT SEEMED TO BE A WHILE BEFORE AMBULANCES ARRIVED

 ALTHOUGH ST JOHN AMBULANCE WERE THERE,

 THEY D I D N ’T HAVE THE FACILITIES TO COPE WITH THE CHAOTIC SITUATION.      I W O U D L N ’T

 PUT ANY BLAME ON THE POLICEMEN INDIVIDUALLY THEY WERE OBVIOUSLY UNDER ORDERS

 AND WERE AWAITING FURTHER INSTRUCTIONS WHICH D I D N ’T SEEM TO, COME.      THE LOUD

 SPEAKER SYSTEM WAS AUDIBLE BUT THE INSTRUCTION SEEMED TO BE NONSENSE, THEY

 WERE ASKING PEOPLE TO GET OFF THE PITCH BUT THERE WAS NO WHERE FOR THEM TO GO.

^pfDICIAL INQUIRY?

 £ “*)WHY WERE THE CROWDS OUTSIDE IN LEPPINGS LANE ALLOWED TO ASSEMBLE WITHOUT

 THE BOTTLE NECK.

 2. WHY WASN'T THE          KICK OFF DELAYED BECAUSE THE POLICE MUST HAVE KNOWN OF

 TRAFFIC DELAYS AND FANS ARRIVING LATE AS SHEFFIELD WAS AT A STANDSTILL.

 3. THE GROUND ENTRANCE DESIGN LEAVES A LOT TO BE DESIRED.          AS 7 TURNSTILES

 IS NOT ENOUGH TO ALLOW FANS ACCESS COMFORTABLY.

 4. THE POLICE COMMUNICATION SYSTEM OBVIOUSLY FAILED BADLY ON THE DAY AND IT

 NEEDS TO B E TOTALLY REVAMPED.
